CARS
["If you're allergic to **** s, this will feel like poison ivy.  So, unless you want a nasty rash across half your body, might best keep perusing threads.\n\nHere's my take on how to surf the big waves without your helmet or knee pads.  I'd love earnest thoughts and opinions on this.\n\nImagine your portfolio is your car.  In this case, mine is an earlier-model Honda Civic.  Maybe an early 90's civic, when Honda made good cars.  If I wreck without insurance, maybe I can limp from the wreck and find a bike.  But bikes suck, and we all know the thought of veering slightly to the side of the road to clip some faggoty Lance-Armstrong-wannabe has crossed our minds at least once.  \n\nIf I find good insurance, though, it doesn't quite replace the well-worn, untarnished gem of a semi-beater I used to drive.  The one I used to bang my wife in, before she got a boyfriend.  Ah, the memories.  But good insurance can be kinda cheap, at least relative to losing everything, and if the worst happens, even shitty insurance will compensate me something that has four wheels, working windows, and the old bumper stickers removed.  I digress.\n\nIt took me a while to arrive here, and I try to learn from every spill, every scab, every raspberry rash still crusty from the jagged asphalt that is the stock market.  So here's what I'm doing.  Again, thoughts welcome.\n\nI have about 30% of my portfolio in long-dated TLT ghetto call spreads.  Long calls are not far OTM, short calls are same expiry, $25 or so farther OTM.  That means, if the markets tank a bit, I'm in the green for at least those, and mostly that's money to me and not the spread.  These spreads for 1/15/2021 cost around $200 apiece right meow, and if we go full circuit-breaker, max payout at expiry is $2500 each.  Not bad.  I'd probably sell them if this happens before though, because like I said, the way those spreads are, I'm probably closing with 50-60% of whatever they're worth at expiry.  This hedge bet does bleed.\n\nFor every $1000 in calls or call spreads I buy, I also pick up one naked VIXY call just above ITM for the same expiry.  If things get nasty just for a day, VIXY is spiky, and decays quickly so I need to exit quickly, but that's the supplemental insurance.  It's not gonna put a spoiler on my shitty little Civic, but it'll replace those headlights that broke on the deer (that 2-day run of down markets that curbed the comeback for a hot minute).\n\nSo far, results have been encouraging.  I'm not trying to make /wsb headlines, but gains have been nice, felt (somewhat) safe, and so far I also haven't had a loss so bad I was obligated by moral imperative to provide pictorial evidence of losing my shirt and half-eaten bag of Skittles.  I've made a few risky bets, won some, lost some.   It's been more fun for me not riding the knife-edge of a day-ruining loss where the knife could go vertical while I'm still sitting on it.\n\nBulltards, do your worst.  I'll be here."]
Bearish: 100 %
Bullish: 0 %
Neutral: 0 %

The one I used to bang my wife in, before she got a boyfriend.  Ah, the memories.  But good insurance can be kinda cheap, at least relative to losing everything, and if the worst happens, even shitty insurance will compensate me something that has four wheels, working windows, and the old bumper stickers removed.  I digress.\n\nIt took me a while to arrive here, and I try to learn from every spill, every scab, every raspberry rash still crusty from the jagged asphalt that is the stock market.  So here's what I'm doing.  Again, thoughts welcome.\n\nI have about 30% of my portfolio in long-dated TLT ghetto call spreads.  Long calls are not far OTM, short calls are same expiry, $25 or so farther OTM.  That means, if the markets tank a bit, I'm in the green for at least those, and mostly that's money to me and not the spread.  These spreads for 1/15/2021 cost around $200 apiece right meow, and if we go full circuit-breaker, max payout at expiry is $2500 each.  Not bad.  I'd probably sell them if this happens before though, because like I said, the way those spreads are, I'm probably closing with 50-60% of whatever they're worth at expiry.  This hedge bet does bleed.\n\nFor every $1000 in calls or call spreads I buy, I also pick up one naked VIXY call just above ITM for the same expiry.  If things get nasty just for a day, VIXY is spiky, and decays quickly so I need to exit quickly, but that's the supplemental insurance.  It's not gonna put a spoiler on my shitty little Civic, but it'll replace those headlights that broke on the deer (that 2-day run of down markets that curbed the comeback for a hot minute).\n\nSo far, results have been encouraging.  I'm not trying to make /wsb headlines, but gains have been nice, felt (somewhat) safe, and so far I also haven't had a loss so bad I was obligated by moral imperative to provide pictorial evidence of losing my shirt and half-eaten bag of Skittles.  I've made a few risky bets, won some, lost some.   It's been more fun for me not riding the knife-edge of a day-ruining loss where the knife could go vertical while I'm still sitting on it.\n\nBulltards, do your worst.  I'll be here."]
Bearish: 100 %
Bullish: 0 %
